| 1:11:45| Yes, and thank you so much to the Mayor and to you, Vice Mayor, and all of the City Council members who have agreed to sign on. I'm grateful.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4305)|
| 1:11:53| I did, Beck has been working on this, as Vice Mayor said, for many years, but I assembled a legal team about two years ago, headed by Attorney Charles Spells, who has been named and included as one of the best lawyers in America when it was first published and for many years thereafter.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4313)|
| 1:12:10| Because I really wanted to look at it from a legal perspective and not just the right thing to do. And I have a seven-page summary from him, of which I will not read, but I would like to share with you just his findings real quickly as a summary.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4330)|
| 1:12:24| And it says, Dear Reverend Kessler, you have asked me to review the trial transcripts, of which Beck has every single court proceeding of the transcripts of Maurice Mays' case.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4344)|
| 1:12:35| In the execution of Knoxville resident Maurice Mays, determined whether he was properly arrested, convicted in a legal proceeding that ignited the great race riot of 1919.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4355)|
| 1:12:46| And he said, for the reasons that follow, I have concluded that Maurice Mays was the victim of a racially motivated, legally improper prosecution that resulted in the execution of an innocent man.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4366)|
| 1:12:57| I won't name all of the names of the persons that also concluded, as Vice Mayor mentioned some of those, but he did conclude his statement that at a time when our nation, our state, and our community continue to struggle to achieve racial justice,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4377)|
| 1:13:11| the prosecution and execution of Maurice Mays continues to haunt the city of Knoxville, and it should.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4391)|
| 1:13:17| One way for the city to obtain a small measure of justice at this late date is to seek once again exoneration for Maurice Mays from the governor,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4397)|
| 1:13:26| who alone has the unfettered right to bring a measure of closure to this tragic case. Exoneration would be a matter of simple racial justice.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4406)|
| 1:13:35| And I think it's fitting, just as I close my remarks, to read something from Maurice Mays himself.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4415)|
| 1:13:40| He wrote a letter to Ms. Parsons with the care of the Center at Nittany Mills, and this was from his national state, Tennessee State Prison at the death chamber.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4420)|
| 1:13:50| The lady who had, the only witness who said he had done this crime, and it says, Dear Ms. Parsons, I humbly beg to write you just the word and plea of your kind consideration.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4430)|
| 1:14:01| While I sit on the brink of the grave, burdened down, I a death cell, waiting the death signal that will send my innocent life into eternity and force me to bid goodbye to this world upon the strength of your word alone.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4441)|
| 1:14:13| I am entirely innocent of the murder of Ms. Lindsay. I truly regret her death as I would any person's.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4453)|
| 1:14:19| I was never at the house which you and Ms. Lindsay lived on or the street which it stood, and I knew nothing whatsoever about the crime until I was told about it after my arrest.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4459)|
| 1:14:29| Ms. Parsons, please, I beg to recall to your memory a mistake of just a few months ago in Knoxville.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4469)|
| 1:14:35| Frank Martian, a colored man, was mistakenly accused by a young white lady who said Martian attacked her and fought her face to face for over 20 minutes in broad daylight on the railroad tracks.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4475)|
| 1:14:47| She was very much mistaken, and her heart was touched by God who looked upon her mistake, and to relieve herself, she corrected her serious mistake that might have meant death for an innocent man.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4487)|
| 1:14:58| Ms. Parsons, please consider she made her mistake in broad daylight. You made your mistake in the nighttime when it was much easier to be mistaken.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4498)|
| 1:15:07| For God's sake, won't you please consider the mistake that calls for taking my innocent life?| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4507)|
| 1:15:12| And at the end of Maurice Mays's life, as he was at the death chamber about to await the death sentence, he prayed this final prayer, which is completely recorded in the black newspapers, of which Beck has.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4512)|
| 1:15:24| And it says, oh, father supreme being, thou who are in above and in all things, I make my final appeal to you, not for my life, but for my soul.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4524)|

| 1:15:43| Bless those thousands who have so nobly stood by me that we now stand in defeat, and forgive those for whom the narrowness of prejudice has placed against me.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4543)|
| 1:15:53| The flash of prejudice has whipped me into the shadows of death.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200728?start=4553)|
